<div>Now, we use the chain rule:</div>

<div>We can simplify this expression:</div>

<div>To find the turning points, we set the derivative equal to zero:</div>

<div>Taking the square root of both sides gives us:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="6.725ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>So, the turning points occur at <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="6.725ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2972.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="2212" d="M84 237T84 250T98 270H679Q694 262 694 250T679 230H98Q84 237 84 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(2472.6, 0)"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>
<div>Now we find the (x,y) coordinates for each value of t:<br>
When <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span><br>
For <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="13.488ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 5961.6 78Q290 50 306 38T341 26Q378 26 414 59T463 140Q466 150 469 151T485 153H489Q504 153 504 145Q504 144 502 134Q486 77 440 33T333 -11Q263 -11 227 52Q186 -10 133 -10H127Q78 -10 57 16T35 71Q35 103 54 123T99 <div>(a) By eliminating the parameter, find the cartesian equation of the curve.</div>
<br>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>The goal of eliminating the parameter is to get a single equation involving only x and y, without t. It’s usually easiest to isolate t from the simpler equation. In this case, equation (2) is perfect for that:</div>
<div>A curve is defined by the parametric equations:<br>

<div>Now, substitute this expression for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.817ex" height="1.441ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -626 361 637"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> into equation (1):</div>

<div>Let’s simplify the expression to get our final Cartesian equation:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -2.148ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="12.031ex" height="5.564ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -1509.9 5317.6 2459.4"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="78" d="M52 tangent to the curve at the point A with parameter <span class="math-inline ">

We want to find the equation of the tangent to this curve at point A, where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>, in the form <span class="math-inline ">

<div>Step 1: Find the coordinates of point A<br>
First, we determine the <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.294ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 572 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="78" d="M52 289Q59 331 106 386T222 442Q257 442 286 424T329 379Q371 442 430 442Q467 442 494 420T522 361Q522 332 508 314T481 292T458 288Q439 288 427 299T415 328Q415 374 465 391Q454 404 425 404Q412 404 406 402Q368 386 350 336Q290 115 290 78Q290 50 306 38T341 26Q378 26 414 59T463 140Q466 150 469 151T485 153H489Q504 153 504 145Q504 144 502 134Q486 77 440 33T333 -11Q263 -11 227 52Q186 -10 133 -10H127Q78 -10 57 16T35 71Q35 103 54 123T99 143Q142 143 142 101Q142 81 130 66T107 46T94 41L91 40Q91 39 97 36T113 29T132 26Q168 26 194 71Q203 87 217 139T245 247T261 313Q266 340 266 352Q266 380 251 392T217 404Q177 404 142 372T93 290Q91 281 88 280T72 278H58Q52 284 52 289Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.464ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.109ex" height="1.464ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 490 647"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="79" d="M21 287Q21 301 36 335T84 406T158 442Q199 442 224 419T250 355Q248 336 247 334Q247 331 231 288T198 191T182 105Q182 62 196 45T238 27Q261 27 281 38T312 61T339 94Q339 95 344 114T358 173T377 247Q415 397 419 404Q432 431 462 431Q475 431 483 424T494 412T496 403Q496 390 447 193T391 -23Q363 -106 294 -155T156 -205Q111 -205 77 -183T43 -117Q43 -95 50 -80T69 -58T89 -48T106 -45Q150 -45 150 -87Q150 -107 138 -122T115 -142T102 -147L99 -148Q101 -153 118 -160T152 -167H160Q177 -167 186 -165Q219 -156 247 -127T290 -65T313 -9T321 21L315 17Q309 13 296 6T270 -6Q250 -11 231 -11Q185 -11 150 11T104 82Q103 89 103 113Q103 170 138 262T173 379Q173 380 173 381Q173 390 173 393T169 400T158 404H154Q131 404 112 385T82 344T65 302T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> coordinates of point A when <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.<br>
Substitute <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> into the parametric equations:<br>
<span class="math-block ">

For parametric equations, we use the chain rule:</div>

<div>Step 5: Convert the equation to the form <span class="math-inline ">

<div>Form the quotient</div>

<br>
<div>(b) Find the cartesian equation of the line segment, stating its domain.</div>
<br>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div><em>Method 1: Eliminate the parameter</em><br>

<br>
<div><em>Method 2: Use the derivative and point-slope form</em><br>
From part (a), we have <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.798ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="9.315ex" height="3.006ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -975.7 4117.3 -45 150 -87Q150 -107 138 -122T115 -142T102 -147L99 -148Q101 -153 118 -160T152 -167H160Q177 -167 186 -165Q219 -156 247 -127T290 -65T313 -9T321 21L315 17Q309 13 296 6T270 -6Q250 -11 231 -11Q185 -11 150 To find the equation of the line, we need a point on the line. We can use <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> to find a point:<br>
When <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>:<br>

<div>So, the point is <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.029ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 2222.7 -141 137 -14T94 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(389, 0)"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 transform="translate(889, 0)"><path data-c="2C" d="M78 35T78 60T94 103T137 121Q165 121 187 96T210 8Q210 -27 201 -60T180 -117T154 -158T130 -185T117 -194Q113 -194 104 -185T95 -172Q95 -168 106 -156T131 -126T157 -76T173 -3V9L172 8Q170 7 167 6T161 3T152 1T140 0Q113 0 96 17Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1333.7, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 725Q56 737 55 738Q55 746 60 749Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>. Using the point-slope form of a line:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18.927ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 8365.6 1000"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="79" d="M21 <div><em>Domain</em><br>
Regarding the domain, since <span class="math-inline ">

<div><span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.452ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="39.367ex" height="2.149ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 17400 950"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="merror"><rect data-background="true" width="17400" height="950" y="-200"></rect><g data-mml-node="mtext"><text data-variant="-explicitFont" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)" font-size="884px">Undefined control sequence \(</text></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>) Show that the equation of the tangent at the point with parameter <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.061ex" height="1.618ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 469 715"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="3B8" d="M35 200Q35 302 74 415T180 610T319 704Q320 704 327 704T339 705Q393 701 423 656Q462 596 462 495Q462 380 417 261T302 66T168 -10H161Q125 -10 99 10T60 63T41 130T35 200ZM383 566Q383 668 330 668Q294 668 260 623T204 521T170 421T157 371Q206 370 254 370L351 371Q352 372 359 404T375 484T383 566ZM113 132Q113 26 166 26Q181 26 198 36T239 74T287 161T335 307L340 324H145Q145 321 136 286T120 208T113 132Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> can be written as <span class="math-inline ">

<div>Point-slope form</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24.537ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>Multiply both sides by \sin\theta</div>

<div>Substitute (<span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="32.019ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 14152.3 <div>Use identity <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="17.665ex" height="2.072ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -833.9 <div>hence the point is</div>

<div>The slope of the tangent is</div>

<div>Thus the slope of the normal is the negative reciprocal:</div>

<ol start="5">
<li><strong>A ball is thrown from a fixed point O on a windy day. At time t seconds after it is thrown, the vertical displacement <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.464ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.109ex" height="1.464ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 490 647"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="79" d="M21 287Q21 301 36 335T84 406T158 442Q199 442 224 419T250 355Q248 336 247 334Q247 331 231 288T198 191T182 105Q182 62 196 45T238 27Q261 27 281 38T312 61T339 94Q339 95 344 114T358 173T377 247Q415 397 419 404Q432 431 462 431Q475 431 483 424T494 412T496 403Q496 390 447 193T391 -23Q363 -106 294 -155T156 -205Q111 -205 77 -183T43 -117Q43 -95 50 -80T69 -58T89 -48T106 -45Q150 -45 150 -87Q150 -107 138 -122T115 -142T102 -147L99 -148Q101 -153 118 -160T152 -167H160Q177 -167 186 -165Q219 -156 247 -127T290 -65T313 -9T321 21L315 17Q309 13 296 6T270 -6Q250 -11 231 -11Q185 -11 150 11T104 82Q103 89 103 113Q103 170 138 262T173 379Q173 380 173 381Q173 390 173 393T169 400T158 404H154Q131 404 112 385T82 344T65 302T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> metres and the horizontal displacement <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.294ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 572 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="78" d="M52 289Q59 331 106 386T222 442Q257 442 286 424T329 379Q371 442 430 442Q467 442 494 420T522 361Q522 332 508 314T481 292T458 288Q439 288 427 299T415 328Q415 374 465 391Q454 404 425 404Q412 404 406 402Q368 386 350 336Q290 115 290 78Q290 50 306 38T341 26Q378 26 414 59T463 140Q466 150 469 151T485 153H489Q504 153 504 145Q504 144 502 134Q486 77 440 33T333 -11Q263 -11 227 52Q186 -10 133 -10H127Q78 -10 57 16T35 71Q35 103 54 123T99 143Q142 143 142 101Q142 81 130 66T107 46T94 41L91 40Q91 39 97 36T113 29T132 26Q168 26 194 71Q203 87 217 139T245 247T261 313Q266 340 266 352Q266 380 251 392T217 404Q177 404 142 372T93 290Q91 281 88 280T72 278H58Q52 284 52 289Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> metres of the ball from <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.05ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.726ex" height="1.643ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -704 763 726"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="4F" d="M740 435Q740 320 676 213T511 42T304 -22Q207 -22 138 35T51 201Q50 209 50 244Q50 346 98 438T227 601Q351 704 476 704Q514 704 524 703Q621 689 680 617T740 435ZM637 476Q637 565 591 615T476 665Q396 665 322 605Q242 542 200 428T157 216Q157 126 200 73T314 19Q404 19 485 98T608 313Q637 408 637 476Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> can be modelled by the parametric equations:</strong></li>

<div>Therefore the position of the ball after <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.05ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.891ex" height="1.557ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 1278 688"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path><path data-c="2E" d="M78 60Q78 84 95 102T138 120Q162 120 180 104T199 61Q199 36 182 18T139 0T96 17T78 60Z" transform="translate(500, 0)"></path><path data-c="38" d="M70 417T70 494T124 618T248 666Q319 666 374 624T429 515Q429 485 418 459T392 417T361 389T335 371T324 363L338 354Q352 344 366 334T382 323Q457 264 457 174Q457 95 399 37T249 -22Q159 -22 101 29T43 155Q43 263 172 335L154 348Q133 361 127 368Q70 417 70 494ZM286 386L292 390Q298 394 301 396T311 403T323 413T334 425T345 438T355 454T364 471T369 491T371 513Q371 556 342 586T275 624Q268 625 242 625Q201 625 165 599T128 534Q128 511 141 492T167 463T217 431Q224 426 228 424L286 386ZM250 21Q308 21 350 55T392 137Q392 154 387 169T375 194T353 216T330 234T301 253T274 270Q260 279 244 289T218 306L210 311Q204 311 181 294T133 239T107 157Q107 98 150 60T250 21Z" transform="translate(778, 0)"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> s is</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.791ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="26.866ex" height="2.713ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>(b) Use this model to find the height of the ball when it has travelled a horizontal distance of 2.25 m</div>

<div>This gives (t=4.5) and (t=0.5). Only (t=0.5) lies in the allowed interval <span class="math-inline ">

Now compute the height:</div>

<div>The height is 3.75 m when the ball has travelled 2.25 m horizontally.</div>
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>
<br>
<div><span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.452ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="39.367ex" height="2.149ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 17400 950"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="merror"><rect data-background="true" width="17400" height="950" y="-200"></rect><g data-mml-node="mtext"><text data-variant="-explicitFont" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)" font-size="884px">Undefined control sequence \(</text></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>) Use this model to find the horizontal displacement of the ball at its maximum height.</div>
<br>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>
<br>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>Find when the height is maximum, then evaluate the horizontal position there.</div>

<div>(d) Explain the significance of the domain of the parametric equations, <span class="math-inline ">

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>t=0 represents the time when the ball is thrown from point O, and t=2 represents the time when the ball lands back on the ground. Therefore, the domain <span class="math-inline ">

<br>
<div>(e) Later in the day, the wind strength increases. It is still blowing from the same direction and the ball is still thrown with the same velocity. Explain how you could refine the model to reflect the change in conditions.</div>
<br>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>Wind strength increase can be modelled by acceleration in the horizontal direction. We can calculate the the starting velocity based on acceleration, and velocity can be used to find the new position in the horizontal direction.<br>
No change in vertical motion.</div>
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>
